FTA has more than 30 New/Small Starts projects in the pipeline; would add 320 mi of transit service to communities that need robust choices.
Over the past decade, 80% of News Starts and Small Starts came in on time and on budget. For projects underway, it will be closer to 90%.
In all, FTA has signed 120 grants for New Starts and 20 for Small Starts &amp; the Obama Admin envisions an even bigger role for the programs.
